What is all this?&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"background: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"background-color: white; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Even as a rubber\nstamp President will you allow this, nonsense ? <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZTGXoHFAu8E/UgtiFVSZr7I/AAAAAAAAlKA/E0-3nGR9jlU/s1600/images.jpgoiung6tr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-ZTGXoHFAu8E/UgtiFVSZr7I/AAAAAAAAlKA/E0-3nGR9jlU/s400/images.jpgoiung6tr.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Let me talk about PERCEPTION first.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Three friends go to a bar for drinking beer ( costing 10\ndollars a bottle ) </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>As usual they take out one 10 dollar bill each from their\nwallets and gives the waiter,<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>3 nos 10\ndollar<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>notes or 30 dollars.</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The bar owner is in a expansive mood and he tells the waiter\n-- \"happy hour time! -- give them 5 dollars back!!-- i will charge only 25\ndollars for 3 beers today \".</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The clever waiter knows 5 dollars cannot be split between 3\nregular dutchmen. so he pockets 2 dollars and returns 3 one dollar notes .</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The three of them put back one dollar each into their\nrespective wallets.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Initially each\nwallet had one 10 dollar bill--now it has only one single dollar bill.</em></span><em><br /></em></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Now comes the perception part:<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /></em><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>All three of them spent 9 dollars each-- 27 dollars total. </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The waiter got 2 dollars.</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">WHERE IS ONE DOLLAR GONE-- POOF???<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Be honest to yourself and dont read further, till you figure\nthis out.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">You tell an accountant without perception to give you a\ndebit/ credit accounts statement--and see the way he sweats. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">See literacy has nothing to do with perception.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>A illiterate chaiwala boy in mumbai can make\nan ass out of you, when it comes to accounts.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Daft accountants make a mistake when it comes to\n\"receipts\" and \" balance \".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Here in this case it is - 30+0= 27+3.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Opening cash + receipts = spent cash+ balance cash.&nbsp; It can\nnever ever be 30-3+2=29</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">See, you cant argue with dorks.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>2 dollars is something which happened in the\nmann mandir of the waiter.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>How do you\nknow that he stole 2 dollars ?<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;\n</span>Accounting has to be objective.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Now let me talk about another case -- It is about RELATIVITY</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">There was this blind man, who used to constantly bitch about\nhis bad luck-- again and again to whoever bothered to listen to him. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Fed up of this broken record,&nbsp;one day a wise man suggested to him, listen I have an\nidea -- let us put you misfortune in a basket, and so will everybody else .&nbsp; Then\nwe will shake up these misfortunes and you can pick up another man's\nmisfortune.&nbsp; You cannot lose as you will gain your eye sight, which you so\nsorely miss.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Before the wise man completed , the blind man told him to\nFO. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">He was happy with his own misfortune.&nbsp; At least he could get a massive hard\non and with that he could enjoy with his girl friend, or all by himself if she\nwas at work, or busy. &nbsp;His girl friend was his fan, as he could sing well and\nand she loved his sense of humor and his performance in bed.&nbsp; And his friends\nhad given him&nbsp;bull&nbsp; that she was attractive, while in reality she looked YUCCKK.</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Suddenly he saw the light,&nbsp; as soon as he related his misfortune with\nanother man's.&nbsp; He never bitched after that.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">So sometimes a leper could be the happier , that a guy in a\nwheel chair with a broken spine.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">It is necessary to compare things in life.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>There are no absolutes like happy, sad, big,\nsmall, beautiful, ugly , strong , weak, rich, poor etc. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">So sometimes when you feel you are happy,&nbsp; it is just your\ncomparison, to what you felt before. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">There has to be a base for every thing.\n&nbsp; Relativity is the only thing which allows anything to exist. this extends from\natoms to living beings to the cosmos.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>There has to be a reference point.&nbsp;&nbsp;People who do NOT understand this\ntruth usually paint themselves into a corner.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">You cant think in black and white. Everything cannot be\ntermed in groups of right and wrong. There are shades of grey. &nbsp;Like President Bush\nsaid, either you are with me or against me.&nbsp; Hey, how about \"who the fu#k are\nyou\" , or h\"ow about a&nbsp;kick on your ass\" ? <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">When dealing with the law you must pinch and remind\nyourself, that absolutes could rule the day. \"Do you plead guity or non-guily\",\nasked the judge.&nbsp; You will piss him off if you say \" I am only a little\nguilty!\" Like the 12 year old girl telling her mother \" Ma, looks like I&nbsp;am a\nlittle pregnant!\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Unlike Hinduism, most modern religions like Christianity ,\nIslam etc are absolute.&nbsp; Members of these religions<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>see their own religion as the one that is right and will regard all\nothers as wrong. Religious intolerance is due to this perception.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">According to the New Testament, the way it reads today\u2019s\nabridged Bible , Jesus Christ said that nobody will be saved except through\nhim.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If the \"Hour of Judgment\"\nwere to take place today, do you truly believe that all non-Christians would be\ndoomed to hell forever?\" A priest will answer this with a huge YES.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Literal and narrow interpretation of holy books as is done\non evangelist TV channels or in a place of worship, can be dangerous. Many\nspiritual statements need to be analyzed and interpreted broadly. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">This is the reason why this planet had to suffer\nInquisitions and crucifications.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Many of\nthe Popes of Vatican were involved in simony, nepotism, torture, murder, sexual\npromiscuity, or other sins unbefitting anyone claim to spread the word of\nGod. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Mahatma Gandhi, had said \"A votary of truth [a person\nfervently devoted to truth] is often obliged to grope in the dark.\"<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Our challenge therefore lies in our blind\nspots, not in our vision.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Unlike\ncorrecting a blind spot in the rear view of an automobile, which can be\nrectified simply by adding a different kind or a supplemental mirror, at\nanother angle, we cannot correct our personal blind spots so easily. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">To correct\nthem, we must grow in our perception and in our acceptance of what is.\n \"Perceive\" means to \"seize wholly,\" to \"see all the\nway through.\" Perception, therefore, is the act of seeing in the mind, of\nunderstanding. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Our perceptions grow and change as we mature, but not\neveryone's perceptions mature at the same rate, which accounts for the widely\ndiffering degrees of consciousness with respect to cause-and-effect\nrelationships, as we see different truths. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HL6CNuwJS_o/UCc6W6JjqrI/AAAAAAAAPic/3Vo02oistJA/s1600/eerggb.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"241\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-HL6CNuwJS_o/UCc6W6JjqrI/AAAAAAAAPic/3Vo02oistJA/s400/eerggb.png\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">So let me quote John Godfrey Saxe's ( 1816-1887) version of\nthe famous Indian legend--the six blind men of Hindoostan-<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>It was six men of Indostan</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>To learning much inclined,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Who went to see the\nElephant</span></span></em></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>(Though all of them were blind),</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>That each by observation</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Might satisfy his mind.</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The First approach'd the Elephant,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>And happening to fall</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Against his broad and sturdy side,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>At once began to bawl:</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>\"God bless me! but the Elephant</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Is very like a wall!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /><span style=\"color: blue;\"></span></em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The Second, feeling of the tusk,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Cried, -\"Ho! what have we here</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>So very round and smooth and sharp?</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>To me 'tis mighty clear</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>This wonder of an Elephant</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Is very like a spear!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /><span style=\"color: blue;\"></span></em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The Third approached the animal,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>And happening to take</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The squirming trunk within his hands,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Thus boldly up and spake:</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>\"I see,\" quoth he, \"the Elephant</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Is very like a snake!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /><span style=\"color: blue;\"></span></em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The Fourth reached out his eager hand,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>And felt about the knee.</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>\"What most this wondrous beast is like</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Is mighty plain,\" quoth he,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>\"'Tis clear enough the Elephant </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Is very like a tree!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /><span style=\"color: blue;\"></span></em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The Fifth, who chanced to touch the ear,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Said: \"E'en the blindest man</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Can tell what this resembles most;</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Deny the fact who can,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>This marvel of an Elephant</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Is very like a fan!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /><span style=\"color: blue;\"></span></em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The Sixth no sooner had begun</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>About the beast to grope,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Then, seizing on the swinging tail</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>That fell within his scope,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>\"I see,\" quoth he, \"the Elephant</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Is very like a rope!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></em></div>\n<em><br /><span style=\"color: blue;\"></span></em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>And so these men of Indostan</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Disputed loud and long,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Each in his own opinion</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Exceeding stiff and strong,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Though each was partly in the right,</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>And all were in the wrong!&nbsp; </em></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">MORAL. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>So oft in theologic wars, </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>The disputants, I ween, </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Rail on in utter ignorance </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Of what each other mean, </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>And prate about an Elephant </em></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><em>Not one of them has seen!</em></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WbfbwhQB43w/UCc6b1udWUI/AAAAAAAAPik/BwvEeMZcBhQ/s1600/ssss.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"258\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WbfbwhQB43w/UCc6b1udWUI/AAAAAAAAPik/BwvEeMZcBhQ/s400/ssss.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Well these were blind men. Let us talk about people who are\nNOT blind. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">The eye sees only what the mind is prepared to comprehend.&nbsp; People see what they want to see and what people want to see\n, never has anything to do with the truth. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Perception determines how a person responds to the\nworld.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>This means there is no\nreality- only perception. This is why people all over the world get fooled by\nclever advertisements and branding. However, the more you already know about a topic, the harder\nit is for anyone to mislead or misinform you.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<em><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\u201cReality is merely an illusion, albeit a very persistent\none.\u201d \u2013 Albert Einstein<o:p></o:p></span></em></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/bwKtihWY_Qs/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/bwKtihWY_Qs&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/bwKtihWY_Qs&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Perception is not always to be trusted, as our perceptions are colored by our beliefs, expectations and\nexperiences. Everything you see or hear or experience in any way at all\nis specific to you. You create a universe by perceiving it, so everything in\nthe universe you perceive is you-specific. You get upset with people as they do NOT conform to your personal rules for the situation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Perception determines reality but at the same time your\n\"perception\" of reality does not mean that it is indeed reality... it is just\nyour reality.</span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Our memories are not the equivalent of video recordings of\nevents. Instead, memories are our interpretative summaries of the information\ngathered by your senses.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Perception is the process of translating the outside world\nto an inside representation into the perceiver.&nbsp; What we perceive as being true is often conditionally true\nrather than empirically true. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Your beliefs, values and references are what make your\nreality.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>You may see a situation as\nbeing bad while a<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>person who is more\noptimistic sees it as an opportunity for growth.&nbsp; One man\u2019s meat is another man\u2019s poison.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>One man\u2019s<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>success is another man\u2019s failure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Business is all about perceptions.&nbsp; The essence of leading, managing, marketing and selling is\ncoming to grips with people's perceptions. There is only one perceived reality, the way each of us\nchooses to perceive a communication, the value of a service, the value of a\nparticular product feature, the quality of a product.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Most of your judgments result from decisional shortcuts and\nthumb rules you use to generate solutions that are good enough most of the\ntime.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>When you perceive a situation\nthat looks familiar to you, doesn't your past experience cause you to see the\nevent in terms of what you expect?<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Doesn't your limited span of attention lead you to categorize things by\naspects that appear similar to what you already know?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">\"We are constantly bombarded with so much sensory\ninformation that it is impossible for us to pay attention to everything.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Our subconscious mind scans our environment\nand selects what it deems may be important for us to notice.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Even then, people not only see things the way\nthey are, they also tend to see what they expect to see, as well as what they\nwant to see.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Much of human perception is\nbased not based on information flowing into the brain from the outside world\n,the brain, based on previous experience, expects to happen next. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Perception is the process of feeling and understanding the\nenvironment by ways of sensory data processing. These sensory data are the\nresults of interactions between sensors and outer stimuli. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Our brains and sense organs are wired in specific ways to\naid in the purpose of survival. This machine is built with specific perceptual\nfunctionality that intentionally orders thought in ways that allow for prime\nsurvival strategies. It doesn\u2019t follow the physical rules or laws of the\nuniverse. It runs with a specific purpose. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Our human machine not only perceives\nthe world, it intentionally creates and re-creates the world around it. It\ndrives and shapes reality even though this would seem to contradict its purpose\nand function. This machine functions through the exploitation of an active\nparadox. It sees what is out there and it creates what it sees. </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Truth is\nabsolute. Perceptions of truth are relative. Therefore, facts, which are\nperceptions of truth, are relative.&nbsp; Paradoxes is something in which the same information may\nlead to two contradictory conclusions--give us pleasure and torment at the same\ntime . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Truth is singular and perceptions plural. The universe functions perfectly . Our perception of how the universe functions is imperfect. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Gandhi had reached this conclusion when he said:<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>\"My aim is not to be consistent with my\nprevious statements, but to be consistent with the truth.&nbsp; The accepted definitions of truth are only modifications of\nthe definitions of perception.&nbsp; Truth as a human understanding resides in everyone's heart,\nand it is there one must search for it. Although we must each be guided by\ntruth as we see it, no one has a right to coerce others to act according to his\nor her own view of truth. In the end, our \"detector of truth\" is our\ninner voice \".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Truth is perfect understanding of that which is. &nbsp;It is\nneither the spoken word nor the written word, although these may have a ring of\ntruth to them. Truth cannot be defined; it can only be experienced and lived. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Truth is universal. Perception of truth is not.&nbsp; Perception in the broadest sense is a matter of interaction\nbetween the world and the self. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">All our knowledge is the offspring of our perceptions.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Attitude can effect perception of the real\nworld and the real world can effect attitude. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Perception is hence more like a reflection of reality than reality\nitself.&nbsp; It is an interpretation of reality that is erroneous\nto some degree and cannot be perfectly correct.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">You can\u2019t touch or feel or see perceived value, yet it\naffects our actions more than we\u2019d like to admit.&nbsp;&nbsp; Knowledge has everything to\ndo with the social acceptability of perception and nothing to do with Truth.&nbsp; Did someone say God Particle ?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">Truth can exist only , only in the present, in this instant,\nin the here and now. The past and the future are both illusions, and like all\nillusions, they are devoid of Truth. &nbsp;Distinguish truth and reality. Truth is is real.&nbsp;&nbsp; Reality is\nnot known, it is realised,experienced.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;\">We're prone to accepting and using all \"shades\" of\ntruth. />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">To rub salt in Gandhiji's wounds , &nbsp;BR Ambedkar was invited again to\nattend the Second Round Table Conference in London in 7th Sept 1931. </span><br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">To divide and rule\nChurchill ( whose mother is Rothschilds ) wanted separate electorate, for lower\ncastes of Hinduism, Islam, Sikhs etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\"><b>The whole idea was to crush Indian freedom movement unity!&nbsp;&nbsp; The white Christian invaders \"divide and rule\" &nbsp;policy at its very best!!</b></span><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Mahatma Gandhi fiercely untouchables would divide the Hindu community into two groups. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: the Yerwada Central Jail of Pune in\n1932 against the separate electorate for untouchables only. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Gandhi's fast provoked huge civil unrest across India, and\northodox Hindu leaders, Congress politicians and activists campaigned .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Such\nwas Gandhiji's mass appeal that Churchill told Ambedkar to call off the game.\nFor if Gandhiji dies, that would mean that the few thousand British invaders\nwould be stoned to death by millions of Indians.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">This agreement, which saw Gandhi end his fast, was called\nthe Poona Pact. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span agreement, Ambedkar dropped the demand for\nseparate electorates that was promised through the British Communal Award prior\nto Ambedkar's meeting with Gandhi. Slavery or\nUntouchability?\u201d</b></span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><strong>Everybody knows both British and Indians that there is not\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">one single instance</span>, in which Ambedkar participated in any activity connected\nwith the struggle to free the country.&nbsp;</strong></span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><strong><br /></strong></span></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><strong>Does anybody want to challenge me?<o:p></o:p></strong></span></span></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;; font-size: large;\"><b>Arun Shourie's spoke the truth ,in his book \u201cWorshipping\nFalse Gods, the Dalit apostle\u201d.&nbsp;</b></span><br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;; font-size: large;\"><b><br /></b></span>\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;; font-size: large;\"><b>In the above book, Arun Shourie described &nbsp;B.R. Ambedkar-- he is portrayed as a\nself-centred, unpatriotic, power-hungry , a stooge of\nthe British.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></b></span><br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>If he arrogantly teaches Brahmanas their duty, the king shall cause hot oil to be poured into his mouth and into his ears.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>With whatever limb a man of a low caste does hurt to (a man of the three) highest (castes), even that limb shall be cut off; that is the teaching of Manu.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>He who raises his hand or a stick, shall have his hand cut off; he who in anger kicks with his foot, shall have his foot cut off.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>A low-caste man who tries to place himself on the same seat with a man of a high caste, shall be branded on his hip and be banished, or (the king) shall cause his buttock to be gashed.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Day and night woman must be kept in dependence by the males (of) their (families), and, if they attach themselves to sensual enjoyments, they must be kept under one\u2019s control.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Her father protects (her) in childhood, her husband protects (her) in youth, and her sons protect (her) in old age; a woman is never fit for independence.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Women must particularly be guarded against evil inclinations, however trifling (they may appear); for, if they are not guarded, they will bring sorrow on two families.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Considering that the highest duty of all castes, even weak husbands (must) strive to guard their wives.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>No man can completely guard women by force; but they can be guarded by the employment of the (following) expedients:<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Let the (husband) employ his (wife) in the collection and expenditure of his wealth, in keeping (everything) clean, in (the fulfillment of) religious duties, in the preparation of his food, and in looking after the household utensils.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Women, confined in the house under trustworthy and obedient servants, are not (well) guarded; but those who of their own accord keep guard over themselves, are well guarded.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Women do not care for beauty, nor is their attention fixed on age; (thinking), \u2018(It is enough that) he is a man,\u2019 they give themselves to the handsome and to the ugly.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>Through their passion for men, through their mutable temper, through their natural heartlessness, they become disloyal towards their husbands, however carefully they may be guarded in this (world).<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>(When creating them) Manu allotted to women (a love of their) bed, (of their) seat and (of) ornament, impure desires, wrath, dishonesty, malice, and bad conduct.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><i>For women no (sacramental) rite (is performed) with sacred texts, thus the law is settled; women (whoare) destitute of strength and destitute of (the knowledge of) Vedic texts, (are as impure as) falsehood (itself), that is a fixed rule.</i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>52.0 %</b></span><br /><br />capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</span></div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0Gvy5mBcipE/WlAJZNfU3zI/AAAAAAABXsU/wZaBJr4cOoclmnshY0dz6Y3NbokDpLaaACK4BGAYYCw/s35/*\" style=\"background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); box-shadow: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1) 1px 1px 5px; max-width: 36px; padding: 5px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c1130910920982097641\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 17.6px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_43M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-PR9PIh5hu24/UCSlIrgthYI/AAAAAAAAPco/5TaOmM405yM/s1600/imagesCCCCC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; </span>10\nmetres off the finish line==for only the beast had a ghost of a chance to run him down.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As the television\ncameras panned each racer, the excitement reached a crescendo when they reached\nBolt in lane seven, dressed in black shorts and the yellow and green singlet of\nthe Jamaican team. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Usain the cool cat he\nis showed no signs of nerves as he bid to replicate his gold medal showing in\nthe Beijing Games in 2008. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He did NOT rob the\nmasses of this planet of their opium. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">To mass delight of\nbillions , he practised his DJ mixing skills, one hand raised to his ear, and\nthen drew laughter after drawing pretend pistols and re holstering them after\npointing them down the track. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-knww_eTuleg/UB9T4FO-_BI/AAAAAAAAPUw/V1KwMBLKmPw/s1600/slide_242838_1333314_free.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"185\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-knww_eTuleg/UB9T4FO-_BI/AAAAAAAAPUw/V1KwMBLKmPw/s320/slide_242838_1333314_free.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As the starter called\nthem to the blocks, Bolt put a finger to his lips to hush the excitable crowd,\nbriefly crossing himself and looking skywards as the television zoomed in and\nhis picture was broadcast on the giant stadium screen.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">As the 8 best\nsuper-sprinters of the planet hunkered down, at the blocks , the electric\ntension in the stadium was palpable\u2014nay \u2013you could cut it with a knife. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When a bottle was thrown from the crowd as Usain settled on the blocks, others were distracted but he did not notice it.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span><o:p></o:p></span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Every Olympic 100m\nchampion in the last 3 decades , had their eyeballs glued on Usain Bolt -\nMaurice Greene, Donovan Bailey, Linford Christie, Carl Lewis , Alan Wells\u2014the lot.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bolt sprinting to the 50\nmetres mark, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>to arrive at his favourite\npart of the race --cheeks puffing, arms pumping right along with each of those\nlengthy strides. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-quto26k5euA/UB9UAkjyaKI/AAAAAAAAPU4/Sjx_4xaRpJA/s1600/s-BOLT-large.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"233\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-quto26k5euA/UB9UAkjyaKI/AAAAAAAAPU4/Sjx_4xaRpJA/s320/s-BOLT-large.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Watch this , Usain now&nbsp;switches on the\ntransition phase--</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pulling away from the pack with every long stride, Bolt\nsurges ahead and overwhelms the star-studded field . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Unlike Beijing , where\nhe show boated the last 20 metres, at London\nhe even dipped at the finish for good measure. The sheer strength of the field\nmeant he could not celebrate from 15 metres out as he had four years ago. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If Beijing was a\nconquest, London was consolidation. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">He had just decimated\nthe star studded field. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-32DPRSxFNEQ/UB9UMRntboI/AAAAAAAAPVA/WbPNqbBt1Lg/s1600/slide_242838_1333298_free.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"245\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-32DPRSxFNEQ/UB9UMRntboI/AAAAAAAAPVA/WbPNqbBt1Lg/s320/slide_242838_1333298_free.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Seven men went under 10\nseconds, beating the previous record of six, achieved at both the 1991 World\nChampionships and 2008 Olympics in Beijing. The times for the athletes\nfinishing from third to seventh were the fastest ever registered for those\npositions. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Had Asafa Powell not\npopped his groin and limped over the line, all eight finalists would have gone\nunder 10 seconds for the first time in history<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"I stopped\nworrying about the start,\" Bolt said. \"The end is what's\nimportant.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After taking half a\nvictory lap around the track, he stopped, kissed the track and gave his\nnow-famous \"To The World\" pose, pointing both fingers in the air, as\nthe denizens of this planet<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>blew their collective\nminds \u2014 the second time after Beijing. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After the finish line, ever the showman, Bolt kept right on running for a victory lap that included high-fives for front-row fans, a pause to crouch down and kiss the track and even a somersault. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The entire 80000 crowd deliriously chanted as one &nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>\"Usain! Usain! Usain!\" . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">What a delectable moment in history.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bolt, as ever, was in the mood for partying - cavorting, clowning, delighting the capacity crowd with his full range of showman celebrations. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p> </o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"People can talk,\" he shrugged afterwards, in a brief moment of sober reflection. \"All they can do is talk. I brought it. I know what I need to do.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">USA's Tyson Gay missed out on the podium, finishing in fourth place at 9.80. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>Gay was in tears following the race. \"I tried maan. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>I tried my best. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span>I just came up short.\"&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"> </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>America still had no answer to Usain\u2019s speed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Bolt now focuses on defending\nhis Beijing gold medals in the 200 meters and 4x100 relay. If he does that,\nhe'll be the first runner in Olympic history to ever defend all three \u201cThat\u2019s\nmy ultimate goal,\" Bolt said of being a legend. \"That's it for\nme.\" <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">His talent was noticed\nearly. . In the absence of a disciplined lifestyle, he became ever-more reliant\non his natural ability to beat back the competition <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>on the track . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Noticing the potential\n, several elite American colleges offered Bolt track scholarships . But the Jamaican\nsmall town boy from Trelawny refused them all, stating that he was content to\nstay in his homeland. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">I had commanded a\nChemical tanker whose home port was Kingston with crew from Jamaica. I spent 6\nmonths of my life there.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>My Jamaican Second\nMate had once told me \u201c Everybody wants to immigrate to America. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>If USA opens out free immigration, the last\nman will have to put off the lights in Jamaica. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Allow\nme to reminisce --<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">At\nBeijing 4 years ago, when Usain Bolt being himself, had showboated, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>immediately his uppity detractors including\nIOC president Jacques Rogge, condemned Bolt and wanted to blackball him and\nstrip him off the gold medal , for showing disrespect. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They\nhad done it in the past for the infamous\" black power salute\", -- to\nJohn Carlos and Tommy Smith ( he smashed the world record in this 200 metres\nevent ) in the 1968 Mexico Olympics. They were on familiar ground.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ghH7_PiEJXs/UB9UV9_X1iI/AAAAAAAAPVI/5pq0GsAM1fk/s1600/jyrterdf.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"199\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ghH7_PiEJXs/UB9UV9_X1iI/AAAAAAAAPVI/5pq0GsAM1fk/s320/jyrterdf.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">This\nwas just a \" human rights salute\" -- misinterpreted to suit the white\nman's mood swings. In that era the black man was an full American with full\nrights and respect only during Olympics-- and that too only the world record\nholders. A devout and articulate black Catholic man could NOT even be a priest.\nThe ball was surely moving this ominous way..<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">How\ndare a mangy black man misbehave in this manner-- only the white Yank like\nsuperbrat John McEnroe can be allowed to get away with this type of bad\nbehaviour, right?.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then\nsomeone had suggested . Usain is now the people's darling. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">There\nwill be riots within the \u201caway from home\u201d Chinese stadium. This Olympics will\nhave to be aborted , if you ever make this silly immature mistake, and you\nmight get a public lynching too. <o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The\npeople of this planet will NOT accept such a gross decision inflicted on this\nliving legend.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Jamaican\nminister Edmund Barlett vigorously supported Bolt , switched himself to wisdom\nmode and opined tersely \" <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The\ncelebrations are appropriate. You have to see the glory of dem moment!\" <o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2YsIpMh5CH4/UB9Uenxbt5I/AAAAAAAAPVQ/zfN5oAbbZ3Y/s1600/slide_242838_1333232_free.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"245\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2YsIpMh5CH4/UB9Uenxbt5I/AAAAAAAAPVQ/zfN5oAbbZ3Y/s320/slide_242838_1333232_free.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue;\">Above- Lightning striking twice!</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">The title of \"world\u2019s\nfastest man\" will continue to remain humanity\u2019s most sought after title.</span> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"color: red;\">Grace and peace!</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;
